## Interface KerMLPackage.Literals

Enclosing interface:
`[KerMLPackage](KerMLPackage.html)`

public static interfaceKerMLPackage.Literals

begin-user-doc 
 Defines literals for the meta objects that represent
 each class,
each feature of each class,
each operation of each class,
each enum,
and each data type
 end-user-doc
